\newcommand{\fontA}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf,+dist,+ccmp}]{Segoe UI Emoji}#1}}
\newcommand{\fontB}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf,+dist,+ccmp}]{Noto Color Emoji}#1}}
\newcommand{\fontC}[1]{{\coloremoji*{#1}}}
\newcommand{\fontD}[1]{{\fontspec[Ligatures=Common,RawFeature={+ccmp}]{Symbola}#1}}
\newcommand{\fontE}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={+ccmp}]{Segoe UI Symbol}#1}}
